<h1 _ngcontent-kxf-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.account.osAccount (系统账号管理)"> @ohos.account.osAccount (系统账号管理) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-kxf-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供管理系统账号的基础能力，包括系统账号的添加、删除、查询、设置、订阅、启动等功能。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1686px;">     <h3 id="checkosaccountactivateddeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">checkOsAccountActivated<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="checkosaccountactivateddeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>checkOsAccountActivated(localId: number, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;boolean&gt;): void</p>     <p>判断指定系统账号是否处于激活状态。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始支持，从API version 11开始废弃。替代方法仅向系统应用开放。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.MANAGE_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS或ohos.permission.INTERACT_ACROSS_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS，以上权限仅系统应用可申请。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.OsAccount</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">localId</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">系统账号ID。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;boolean&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。返回true表示账号已激活；返回false表示账号未激活。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-account">账号管理错误码</a>和<a <p>判断指定系统账号是否具有指定约束。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始支持，从API version 11开始废弃。替代方法仅向系统应用开放。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.MANAGE_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS或ohos.permission.INTERACT_ACROSS_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS，以上权限仅系统应用可申请。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> <p>检查指定系统账号是否已验证。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始支持，从API version 11开始废弃。替代方法仅向系统应用开放。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.MANAGE_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS或ohos.permission.INTERACT_ACROSS_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS，以上权限仅系统应用可申请。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>checkOsAccountVerified(localId: number): Promise&lt;boolean&gt;</p>     <p>检查指定系统账号是否已验证。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始支持，从API version 11开始废弃。替代方法仅向系统应用开放。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.MANAGE_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS或ohos.permission.INTERACT_ACROSS_LOCAL_ACCOUNTS，以上权限仅系统应用可申请。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">localId</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">系统账号ID。不填则检查当前系统账号是否已验证。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。返回true表示当前账号已认证解锁；返回false表示当前账号未认证解锁。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1449px;">     <h3 id="getaccountserverconfig18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getAccountServerConfig<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getaccountserverconfig18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getAccountServerConfig(domainAccountInfo: DomainAccountInfo): Promise&lt;DomainServerConfig&gt;</p>     <p>获取目标域账号的服务器配置。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Account.OsAccount</p>     <p><strong>需要权限：</strong> ohos.permission.MANAGE_DOMAIN_ACCOUNT_SERVER_CONFIGS</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">domainAccountInfo</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a
